 grih mantralay ke ek varisht adhikari ne kaha, ‚Äò‚Äòyadhyapi suraksha ke mudde hai, kisi bhi aagatuk ke liye sanchaar mahatvapurn he

 ‚Äô‚Äôtippaniyan As part of the proposal, the Ministry of Tourism is planning to present a kit which includes, among other things, a SIM card, map, booklets and cds containing information about various tourist destinations, guidelines on what to do and what not to do

 Jenny Radesky, the study's top author from Boston University School of Medicine, said, 'technology is developing rapidly for your young children
 yah adhyayan bal chikitsa pradaataaon ko mata-pitaaon ke anubhavon or chintaaon ko samajhane main madad karata he

 in sabaki ausat umr 38 varsh thi

 adhyayan ke parinaam darshaate hai ki abhibhavakon ko praudyogiki ko lekar kaaphi tanaav he

 unke bachche nau saal se kam umr ke hai
 The results of the study indicate that parents are highly stressed about technology

 is
 aapane aksar logon ko ye kehete suna hoga ki urine rokna swasthya ke liye nuksaandeh hota he

 urine ko ek se do ghante tak rokane se kai tarah kii samasyaayein ho jaati he
